	[BODY:HUMANOID_ARMLESS_NECK:2WINGS:2EYES:2LUNGS:HEART:GUTS:ORGANS:GIZZARD:HUMANOID_JOINTS:THROAT:NECK:SPINE:BRAIN:SKULL:4TOES:BEAK:RIBCAGE]

	[BODY_APPEARANCE_MODIFIER:BROADNESS:90:95:98:100:102:105:110]

	[CASTE:FEMALE]
		[FEMALE]
		[DESCRIPTION:A tiny, carrion-feeding bird with black, almost glossy feathers and an inquisitive, intelligent nature.  She can be noisy, especially when joined by flocks of her kind.]{+}
		[LAYS_EGGS]
			[EGG_MATERIAL:LOCAL_CREATURE_MAT:EGGSHELL:SOLID]
			[EGG_MATERIAL:LOCAL_CREATURE_MAT:EGG_WHITE:LIQUID]
			[EGG_MATERIAL:LOCAL_CREATURE_MAT:EGG_YOLK:LIQUID]
			[EGG_SIZE:21]
			[CLUTCH_SIZE:4:6]
	[CASTE:MALE]
		[MALE]
		[DESCRIPTION:A tiny, carrion-feeding bird with black, almost glossy feathers and an inquisitive, intelligent nature.  He can be noisy, especially when joined by flocks of his kind.]{+}
	[SELECT_CASTE:ALL]
		[SET_TL_GROUP:BY_CATEGORY:ALL:FEATHER]
			[TL_COLOR_MODIFIER:BLACK:1]
				[TLCM_NOUN:feathers:PLURAL]
		[SET_TL_GROUP:BY_CATEGORY:BEAK:BONE]{+  Revision: describe crow beaks as black.}
			[TL_COLOR_MODIFIER:BLACK:1]
				[TLCM_NOUN:beak:SINGULAR]
		[SET_TL_GROUP:BY_CATEGORY:ALL:SKIN]
	[TL_COLOR_MODIFIER:BROWN:1:BURNT_UMBER:1:CINNAMON:1:COPPER:1:DARK_BROWN:1:DARK_PEACH:1:DARK_TAN:1:ECRU:1:PALE_BROWN:1:PALE_CHESTNUT:1:PALE_PINK:1:PEACH:1:PINK:1:RAW_UMBER:1:SEPIA:1:TAN:1:TAUPE_PALE:1:TAUPE_SANDY:1]
				[TLCM_NOUN:skin:SINGULAR]
		[SET_TL_GROUP:BY_CATEGORY:EYE:EYE]
			[TL_COLOR_MODIFIER:BLACK:1]
				[TLCM_NOUN:eyes:PLURAL]

[CREATURE:CROW_MAN]
	[COPY_TAGS_FROM:BIRD_CROW]
	[APPLY_CREATURE_VARIATION:ANIMAL_PERSON]
	[APPLY_CREATURE_VARIATION:RENAME_LEATHER_TO:FEATHER]{+  Revision: the leather is still feathery after tanning.}
	[GO_TO_END]
	[SELECT_CASTE:MALE]
		[CASTE_NAME:crow harp:crow harps:crow harp]{:crow man:crow men:crow man}
		[DESCRIPTION:A small, naked, and feathery man with broad, enveloping wings on his back and a long beak.  His black, almost glossy feathers are longer around his neck, forming a kind of scarf.  He has a shadowy appearance except for where his feathers thin, showing skin.]{+}
	[SELECT_CASTE:FEMALE]
		[CASTE_NAME:crow harpy:crow harpies:crow harpy]{:crow woman:crow women:crow woman}
		[DESCRIPTION:A small, naked, and feathery woman with broad, enveloping wings on her back and a long beak.  Her black, almost glossy feathers are longer around her neck, forming a kind of scarf.  She has a shadowy appearance except for where her feathers thin, showing skin.]{+}
	[SELECT_CASTE:ALL]
	[APPLY_CREATURE_VARIATION:PUNCH_ATTACK]
	[APPLY_CREATURE_VARIATION:TALON_KICK_ATTACK]{:KICK_ATTACK  Revision: combined the talon scratch and kick attacks.}
	{APPLY_CREATURE_VARIATION:TALON_SCRATCH_ATTACK}
	[APPLY_CREATURE_VARIATION:BEAK_BITE_ATTACK]
	[APPLY_CREATURE_VARIATION:STANDARD_BIPED_GAITS:900:750:600:439:1900:2900] 20 kph
	[APPLY_CREATURE_VARIATION:STANDARD_FLYING_GAITS:900:691:482:251:1900:2900] 35 kph
	[APPLY_CREATURE_VARIATION:STANDARD_CLIMBING_GAITS:2990:2257:1525:731:4300:6100] 12 kph
	[APPLY_CREATURE_VARIATION:STANDARD_SWIMMING_GAITS:2990:2257:1525:731:4300:6100] 12 kph
	[APPLY_CREATURE_VARIATION:STANDARD_CRAWLING_GAITS:2990:2257:1525:731:4300:6100] 12 kph
	[GO_TO_START]
	[NAME:crow harpy:crow harpies:crow harpy]{:crow man:crow men:crow man}
	[DESCRIPTION:A small person with the head and wings of a crow.]
	[POPULATION_NUMBER:5:10]
	[CLUSTER_NUMBER:5:10]
	[MAXAGE:60:80]

		[DESCRIPTION:A large, inquisitive bird with black, almost glossy feathers and an ominous, echoing call.  She scavenges for food and carrion, tearing flesh with her long beak.]{+}

		[DESCRIPTION:A large, inquisitive bird with black, almost glossy feathers and an ominous, echoing call.  He scavenges for food and carrion, tearing flesh with his long beak.]{+}
	[SELECT_CASTE:ALL]
	[CHANGE_BODY_SIZE_PERC:40700]
	[GO_TO_START]
